Coordinates increase right and down.\n+pub const Rect = struct {\n+    x: u16,\n+    y: u16,\n+    width: u16,\n+    height: u16,\n+\n+    pub fn init(x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, height: u16) Rect {\n+        return .{ .x = x, .y = y, .width = width, .height = height };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns a new Rect inset by `margin` on all sides.\n+    /// Uses saturating subtraction to prevent underflow.\n+    /// Position shifts inward; dimensions shrink by 2*margin (or to zero).\n+    pub fn inner(self: Rect, margin: u16) Rect {\n+        const double_margin = @as(u32, margin) * 2;\n+\n+        return .{\n+            .x = self.x +| margin,\n+            .y = self.y +| margin,\n+            .width = if (double_margin >= self.width) 0 else self.width - @as(u16, @intCast(double_margin)),\n+            .height = if (double_margin >= self.height) 0 else self.height - @as(u16, @intCast(double_margin)),\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns area (width * height) as u32 to prevent overflow.\n+    pub fn area(self: Rect) u32 {\n+        return @as(u32, self.width) * @as(u32, self.height);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns true if rect has zero area.\n+    pub fn isEmpty(self: Rect) bool {\n+        return self.width == 0 or self.height == 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Clamp a point to be within this rect (inclusive of boundaries).\n+    /// Returns the closest point inside the rect.\n+    pub fn clamp(self: Rect, x: u16, y: u16) Position {\n+        const max_x = self.x +| (self.width -| 1);\n+        const max_y = self.y +| (self.height -| 1);\n+\n+        return .{\n+            .x = std.math.clamp(x, self.x, max_x),\n+            .y = std.math.clamp(y, self.y, max_y),\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns the right edge x coordinate (exclusive).\n+    pub fn right(self: Rect) u16 {\n+        return self.x +| self.width;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns the bottom edge y coordinate (exclusive).\n+    pub fn bottom(self: Rect) u16 {\n+        return self.y +| self.height;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns true if the given point is within this rect (inclusive).\n+    pub fn contains(self: Rect, x: u16, y: u16) bool {\n+        return x >= self.x and\n+            x < self.right() and\n+            y >= self.y and\n+            y < self.bottom();\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// +1,203 @@\n+// Layout types for zithril TUI framework\n+// Constraint-based layout system inspired by ratatui\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+\n+/// Direction for layout: how children are arranged.\n+pub const Direction = enum {\n+    horizontal,\n+    vertical,\n+};\n+\n+/// Constraints describe how space should be allocated among layout children.\n+///\n+/// The constraint solver allocates space in this order:\n+/// 1. Fixed constraints (length): Allocate exact requested size\n+/// 2. Minimum constraints (min): Allocate at least requested size\n+/// 3. Maximum constraints (max): Allocate at most requested size\n+/// 4. Ratio constraints (ratio): Allocate fraction of total space\n+/// 5. Flex constraints (flex): Distribute remaining space proportionally\n+///\n+/// When space is insufficient:\n+/// - Fixed/min constraints take priority\n+/// - Flex items shrink to zero before fixed items shrink\n+/// - No negative sizes (saturating arithmetic)\n+pub const Constraint = union(enum) {\n+    /// Exactly n cells.\n+    length: u16,\n+\n+    /// At least n cells.\n+    min: u16,\n+\n+    /// At most n cells.\n+    max: u16,\n+\n+    /// Fraction of available space (numerator, denominator).\n+    /// Example: ratio(1, 3) means 1/3 of available space.\n+    ratio: Ratio,\n+\n+    /// Proportional share (like CSS flex-grow).\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(1) = 50/50 split\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(2) = 33/67 split\n+    flex: u16,\n+\n+    pub const Ratio = struct {\n+        num: u16,\n+        den: u16,\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Create a length constraint (exactly n cells).\n+    pub fn len(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .length = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a minimum constraint (at least n cells).\n+    pub fn minSize(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .min = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a maximum constraint (at most n cells).\n+    pub fn maxSize(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .max = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a ratio constraint (num/den of available space).\n+    pub fn fractional(num: u16, den: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .ratio = .{ .num = num, .den = den } };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a flex constraint (proportional share).\n+    pub fn flexible(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .flex = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Apply this constraint to resolve a concrete size given available space.\n+    /// Returns the size this constraint requests, which may exceed available space.\n+    /// The caller is responsible for ensuring the total doesn't exceed available.\n+    pub fn apply(self: Constraint, available: u16) u16 {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .length => |n| n,\n+            .min => |n| n,\n+            .max => |n| @min(n, available),\n+            .ratio => |r| blk: {\n+                if (r.den == 0) break :blk 0;\n+                const result = (@as(u32, available) * @as(u32, r.num)) / @as(u32, r.den);\n+                break :blk @intCast(@min(result, available));\n+            },\n+            .flex => available,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if two constraints are equal.\n+    pub fn eql(self: Constraint, other: Constraint) bool {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .length => |n| other == .length and other.length == n,\n+            .min => |n| other == .min and other.min == n,\n+            .max => |n| other == .max and other.max == n,\n+            .ratio => |r| other == .ratio and other.ratio.num == r.num and other.ratio.den == r.den,\n+            .flex => |n| other == .flex and other.flex == n,\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.len creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.len(10);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .length);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), c.length);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.minSize creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(20);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .min);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), c.min);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.maxSize creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(30);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .max);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.max);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.fractional creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 3);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .ratio);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), c.ratio.num);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 3), c.ratio.den);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.flexible creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(2);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .flex);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 2), c.flex);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Direction enum values\" {\n+    try std.testing.expect(@intFromEnum(Direction.horizontal) != @intFromEnum(Direction.vertical));\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Constraint application\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint length apply returns exact size\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.len(50);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(30));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint min apply returns minimum size\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(30);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(20));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint max apply caps at available\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(50);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(30));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint ratio apply calculates fraction\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 4);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 25), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(200));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint ratio apply handles zero denominator\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 0);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(100));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint flex apply returns full available\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(1);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 100), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(0));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint eql checks equality\" {\n+    try std.testing.expect(Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.len(10)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.len(20)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.minSize(10)));\n+\n+    try std.testing.expect(Constraint.fractional(1, 3).eql(Constraint.fractional(1, 3)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.fractional(1, 3).eql(Constraint.fractional(2, 3)));\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// REGRESSION TESTS - Edge cases\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"regression: Constraint ratio with large values doesn't overflow\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(65535, 2);\n+    const result = c.apply(65535);\n+    try std.testing.expect(result <= 65535);\n+}\n+\n+test \"regression: Constraint max with zero available\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(100);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(0));\n+}\ndiff --git a/src/main.zig b/src/main.zig\nindex 9647d10..3eec6a7 100644\n--- a/src/main.zig\n+++ b/src/main.zig\n@@ -18,17 +18,31 @@ pub fn -0,0 +1,338 @@\n+// Style types for zithril TUI framework\n+// Re-exports and extends rich_zig's Style with zithril-specific conveniences\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+pub const rich_zig = @import(\"rich_zig\");\n+\n+/// Re-export rich_zig's Color for convenience.\n+pub const Color = rich_zig.Color;\n+\n+/// Re-export rich_zig's StyleAttribute for convenience.\n+pub const StyleAttribute = rich_zig.StyleAttribute;\n+\n+/// Style represents visual attributes for text cells.\n+///\n+/// Wraps rich_zig.Style with zithril-specific conveniences.\n+/// Supports:\n+/// - Foreground and background colors (via Color)\n+/// - Text attributes: bold, italic, underline, dim, blink, reverse, strikethrough\n+/// - Method chaining for building styles\n+/// - Merging styles via patch() (called combine() in rich_zig)\n+///\n+/// Example:\n+/// ```\n+/// const highlight = Style.init().bold().fg(.yellow).bg(.blue);\n+/// const merged = base_style.patch(highlight);\n+/// ```\n+pub const Style = struct {\n+    inner: rich_zig.Style,\n+\n+    /// Empty style with all defaults.\n+    pub const empty: Style = .{ .inner = rich_zig.Style.empty };\n+\n+    /// Initialize an empty style.\n+    pub fn init() Style {\n+        return empty;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set foreground color.\n+    pub fn fg(self: Style, c: Color) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.fg(c) };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set foreground color (alias for fg).\n+    pub fn foreground(self: Style, c: Color) Style {\n+        return self.fg(c);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set background color.\n+    pub fn bg(self: Style, c: Color) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.bg(c) };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set background color (alias for bg).\n+    pub fn background(self: Style, c: Color) Style {\n+        return self.bg(c);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable bold.\n+    pub fn bold(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.bold() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable bold.\n+    pub fn notBold(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notBold() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable italic.\n+    pub fn italic(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.italic() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable italic.\n+    pub fn notItalic(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notItalic() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable underline.\n+    pub fn underline(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.underline() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable underline.\n+    pub fn notUnderline(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notUnderline() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable dim.\n+    pub fn dim(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.dim() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable dim.\n+    pub fn self.inner.blink() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable blink.\n+    pub fn notBlink(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notBlink() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable reverse video.\n+    pub fn reverse(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.reverse() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable reverse video.\n+    pub fn notReverse(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notReverse() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable strikethrough.\n+    pub fn strikethrough(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.strikethrough() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Disable strikethrough.\n+    pub fn notStrikethrough(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notStrike() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable strikethrough (alias).\n+    pub fn strike(self: Style) Style {\n+        return self.strikethrough();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Merge another style on top of this one.\n+    /// Non-default values in `other` override values in `self`.\n+    pub fn patch(self: Style, other: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.combine(other.inner) };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Merge another style on top of this one (alias for patch).\n+    pub fn combine(self: Style, other: Style) Style {\n+        return self.patch(other);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if style has a specific attribute enabled.\n+    pub fn hasAttribute(self: Style, attr: return self.inner.isEmpty();\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check equality with another style.\n+    pub fn eql(self: Style, other: Style) bool {\n+        return self.inner.eql(other.inner);\n+    }\n+\n+ @import(\"std\");\n+\n+/// Simple x,y coordinate pair in terminal space.\n+/// Origin (0,0) is top-left of terminal/region.\n+pub const Position = struct {\n+    x: u16,\n+    y: u16,\n+\n+    pub fn init(x: u16, y: u16) Position {\n+        return .{ .x = x, .y = y };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+/// Represents a rectangular region in terminal coordinates.\n+/// Origin (0,0) is top-left. Coordinates increase right and down.\n+pub const Rect = struct {\n+    x: u16,\n+    y: u16,\n+    width: u16,\n+    height: u16,\n+\n+    pub fn init(x: u16, y: u16, width: u16, height: u16) Rect {\n+        return .{ .x = x, .y = y, .width = width, .height = height };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns a new Rect inset by `margin` on all sides.\n+    /// Uses saturating subtraction to prevent underflow.\n+    /// Position shifts inward; dimensions shrink by 2*margin (or to zero).\n+    pub fn inner(self: Rect, margin: u16) Rect {\n+        const double_margin = @as(u32, margin) * 2;\n+\n+        return .{\n+            .x = self.x +| margin,\n+            .y = self.y +| margin,\n+            .width = if (double_margin >= self.width) 0 else self.width - @as(u16, @intCast(double_margin)),\n+            .height = if (double_margin >= self.height) 0 else self.height - @as(u16, @intCast(double_margin)),\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns area (width * height) as u32 to prevent overflow.\n+    pub fn area(self: Rect) u32 {\n+        return @as(u32, self.width) * @as(u32, self.height);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns true if rect has zero area.\n+    pub fn isEmpty(self: Rect) bool {\n+        return self.width == 0 or self.height == 0;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Clamp a point to be within this rect (inclusive of boundaries).\n+    /// Returns the closest point inside the rect.\n+    pub fn clamp(self: Rect, x: u16, y: u16) Position {\n+        const max_x = self.x +| (self.width -| 1);\n+        const max_y = self.y +| (self.height -| 1);\n+\n+        return .{\n+            .x = std.math.clamp(x, self.x, max_x),\n+            .y = std.math.clamp(y, self.y, max_y),\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns the right edge x coordinate (exclusive).\n+    pub fn right(self: Rect) u16 {\n+        return self.x +| self.width;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns the bottom edge y coordinate (exclusive).\n+    pub fn bottom(self: Rect) u16 {\n+        return self.y +| self.height;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Returns true if the given point is within this rect (inclusive).\n+    pub fn contains(self: Rect, x: u16, y: u16) bool {\n+        return x >= self.x and\n+            x < self.right() and\n+            y >= self.y and\n+            y < self.bottom();\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// +1,203 @@\n+// Layout types for zithril TUI framework\n+// Constraint-based layout system inspired by ratatui\n+\n+const std = @import(\"std\");\n+\n+/// Direction for layout: how children are arranged.\n+pub const Direction = enum {\n+    horizontal,\n+    vertical,\n+};\n+\n+/// Constraints describe how space should be allocated among layout children.\n+///\n+/// The constraint solver allocates space in this order:\n+/// 1. Fixed constraints (length): Allocate exact requested size\n+/// 2. Minimum constraints (min): Allocate at least requested size\n+/// 3. Maximum constraints (max): Allocate at most requested size\n+/// 4. Ratio constraints (ratio): Allocate fraction of total space\n+/// 5. Flex constraints (flex): Distribute remaining space proportionally\n+///\n+/// When space is insufficient:\n+/// - Fixed/min constraints take priority\n+/// - Flex items shrink to zero before fixed items shrink\n+/// - No negative sizes (saturating arithmetic)\n+pub const Constraint = union(enum) {\n+    /// Exactly n cells.\n+    length: u16,\n+\n+    /// At least n cells.\n+    min: u16,\n+\n+    /// At most n cells.\n+    max: u16,\n+\n+    /// Fraction of available space (numerator, denominator).\n+    /// Example: ratio(1, 3) means 1/3 of available space.\n+    ratio: Ratio,\n+\n+    /// Proportional share (like CSS flex-grow).\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(1) = 50/50 split\n+    /// flex(1) and flex(2) = 33/67 split\n+    flex: u16,\n+\n+    pub const Ratio = struct {\n+        num: u16,\n+        den: u16,\n+    };\n+\n+    /// Create a length constraint (exactly n cells).\n+    pub fn len(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .length = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a minimum constraint (at least n cells).\n+    pub fn minSize(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .min = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a maximum constraint (at most n cells).\n+    pub fn maxSize(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .max = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a ratio constraint (num/den of available space).\n+    pub fn fractional(num: u16, den: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .ratio = .{ .num = num, .den = den } };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Create a flex constraint (proportional share).\n+    pub fn flexible(n: u16) Constraint {\n+        return .{ .flex = n };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Apply this constraint to resolve a concrete size given available space.\n+    /// Returns the size this constraint requests, which may exceed available space.\n+    /// The caller is responsible for ensuring the total doesn't exceed available.\n+    pub fn apply(self: Constraint, available: u16) u16 {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .length => |n| n,\n+            .min => |n| n,\n+            .max => |n| @min(n, available),\n+            .ratio => |r| blk: {\n+                if (r.den == 0) break :blk 0;\n+                const result = (@as(u32, available) * @as(u32, r.num)) / @as(u32, r.den);\n+                break :blk @intCast(@min(result, available));\n+            },\n+            .flex => available,\n+        };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Check if two constraints are equal.\n+    pub fn eql(self: Constraint, other: Constraint) bool {\n+        return switch (self) {\n+            .length => |n| other == .length and other.length == n,\n+            .min => |n| other == .min and other.min == n,\n+            .max => |n| other == .max and other.max == n,\n+            .ratio => |r| other == .ratio and other.ratio.num == r.num and other.ratio.den == r.den,\n+            .flex => |n| other == .flex and other.flex == n,\n+        };\n+    }\n+};\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// SANITY TESTS - Basic functionality\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.len creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.len(10);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .length);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 10), c.length);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.minSize creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(20);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .min);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 20), c.min);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.maxSize creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(30);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .max);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.max);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.fractional creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 3);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .ratio);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 1), c.ratio.num);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 3), c.ratio.den);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Constraint.flexible creates correct constraint\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(2);\n+    try std.testing.expect(c == .flex);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 2), c.flex);\n+}\n+\n+test \"sanity: Direction enum values\" {\n+    try std.testing.expect(@intFromEnum(Direction.horizontal) != @intFromEnum(Direction.vertical));\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// BEHAVIOR TESTS - Constraint application\n+// ============================================================\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint length apply returns exact size\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.len(50);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(30));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint min apply returns minimum size\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.minSize(30);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(20));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint max apply caps at available\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.maxSize(50);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 30), c.apply(30));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint ratio apply calculates fraction\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 4);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 25), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 50), c.apply(200));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint ratio apply handles zero denominator\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.fractional(1, 0);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(100));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint flex apply returns full available\" {\n+    const c = Constraint.flexible(1);\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 100), c.apply(100));\n+    try std.testing.expectEqual(@as(u16, 0), c.apply(0));\n+}\n+\n+test \"behavior: Constraint eql checks equality\" {\n+    try std.testing.expect(Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.len(10)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.len(20)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.len(10).eql(Constraint.minSize(10)));\n+\n+    try std.testing.expect(Constraint.fractional(1, 3).eql(Constraint.fractional(1, 3)));\n+    try std.testing.expect(!Constraint.fractional(1, 3).eql(Constraint.fractional(2, 3)));\n+}\n+\n+// ============================================================\n+// REGRESSION TESTS - Edge cases\n+// (called combine() in rich_zig)\n+///\n+/// Example:\n+/// ```\n+/// const highlight = Style.init().bold().fg(.yellow).bg(.blue);\n+/// const merged = base_style.patch(highlight);\n+/// ```\n+pub const   pub fn init() Style {\n+        return empty;\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set foreground color.\n+    pub fn fg(self: Style, c: Color) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.fg(c) };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set foreground color (alias for fg).\n+    pub fn foreground(self: Style, c: Color) Style {\n+        return self.fg(c);\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Set background color.\n+    pub fn bg(self: Style,   }\n+\n+    /// Disable italic.\n+    pub fn notItalic(self: Style) Style {\n+        return .{ .inner = self.inner.notItalic() };\n+    }\n+\n+    /// Enable underline.\n+    pub fn underline(self:
